***размещение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a> (12352)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разместить.html>размести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razmestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razmeščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>placing, placement
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мебель.html>ме́бели</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> mébeli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the placement of furniture</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:груз.html>гру́за</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> grúza</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stowage</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>accommodation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:номер.html>но́мер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> одноме́стным (двухме́стным) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́нием</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nómer s odnoméstnym (dvuxméstnym) <b>razmeščénijem</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">single (double) room</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́рам</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>во́йск</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> po kvartíram (vojsk)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">quartering; billeting</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>deployment, stationing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вооруженный.html>вооружённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> vooružónnyx sil</i> ― <span class="e-translation">deployment/stationing of armed forces</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ракета.html>раке́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> rakét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">deployment of missiles</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>placement, layout; distribution pattern
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:население.html>населе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> naselénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">population distribution</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:предприятие.html>предприя́тий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> predprijátij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">placement/distribution of enterprises</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finances</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> placement
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:капитал.html>капита́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> kapitála</i> ― <span class="e-translation">investment</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> за́йма</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> zájma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">distributing/floating a loan</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ценный.html>це́нных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razmeščénije</b> cénnyx bumág</i> ― <span class="e-translation">placement of securities</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начальный.html>нача́льное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:публичный.html>публи́чное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:размещение.html>размеще́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">načálʹnoje publíčnoje <b>razmeščénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">initial public offering (IPO)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разминать.html>размина́ть</a> (16067)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мина́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-minátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разминать.html>размина́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razminátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размять.html>размя́ть</a></b>)

<li>to mash</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stretch (one's legs, muscles, etc.)</li></ol>

***размножение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:размножение.html>размноже́ние</a> (18140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размножение.html>размноже́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razmnožénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размножение.html>размноже́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размножение.html>размноже́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размножение.html>размноже́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reproduction (<i>the act of reproducing new individuals biologically</i>), breeding
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:размножение.html>размноже́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бактерия.html>бакте́рий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a> уско́рилось <a href = vnd.unilang:вдвое.html>вдво́е</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Razmnožénije</b> baktérij/baktɛ́rij za god uskórilosʹ vdvóje.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Reproduction rate of bacteria increased twofold in a year.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>propagation, duplication</li></ol>

***размотать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:размотать.html>размота́ть</a> (18959)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мотать.html>мота́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">motátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размотать.html>размота́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razmotátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разматывать.html>разма́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to unwind, to unreel</li></ol>

***размягчить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:размягчить.html>размягчи́ть</a> (25406)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мягчи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjaxčítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>to soften</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mellow, to melt, to disarm <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of emotion</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мять.html>мя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:размять.html>размя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razmjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разминать.html>размина́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to knead
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мять.html>мять</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разминать.html>размина́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razminátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to mash</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stretch (one's legs, muscles, etc.)</li></ol>

***разнести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разнести.html>разнести́</a> (7900)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разнести.html>разнести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raznestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разносить.html>разноси́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to carry, to convey, to deliver</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(news, rumor etc)</i> to spread around</li>
<li>to enter, to book</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause to swell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёку</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разнести.html>разнесло́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú ščóku <b>raznesló</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his cheek is swollen</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разнести.html>разнесло́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>raznesló</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has grown round/rotund/lumpish</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to smash, to destroy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разнести.html>разнести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:щепка.html>ще́пки</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кусок.html>куски́</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raznestí</b> v ščépki (na kuskí)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break/smash to pieces</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scatter, to disperse
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разнести.html>разнёс</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обрывок.html>обры́вки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">véter <b>raznjós</b> obrývki bumági</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wind scattered scraps of paper</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give a rating/dressing-down, to dress down, to blow up</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разноситься.html>разноси́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raznosítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разнестись.html>разнести́сь</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raznestísʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***разнимать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разнимать.html>разнима́ть</a> (23372)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разнимать.html>разнима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raznimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разнять.html>разня́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разница.html>ра́зница</a> (1824)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разный.html>ра́зный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ráznyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ица</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разница.html>ра́зница</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ráznica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разница.html>ра́зницы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разница.html>ра́зницы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разница.html>ра́зниц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>difference (quality of being different, can be used to refer to the difference itself without talking about its size)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разница.html>ра́зница</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возраст.html>во́зрасте</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ráznica</b> v vózraste</i> ― <span class="e-translation">age difference</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***разногласие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разногласие.html>разногла́сие</a> (12826)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разный.html>ра́зный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ráznyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глас.html>глас</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glas</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разногласие.html>разногла́сие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raznoglásije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разногласие.html>разногла́сия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разногласие.html>разногла́сия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разногласие.html>разногла́сий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>difference, disagreement, discord
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>ни́ми</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разногласие.html>разногла́сия</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">méždu ními <b>raznoglásija</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">they are at variance; they are in disagreement</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разногласие.html>разногла́сие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взгляд.html>взгля́дах</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raznoglásije</b> vo vzgljádax</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">difference of opinion</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устранить.html>устрани́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разногласие.html>разногла́сия</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ustranítʹ <b>raznoglásija</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to settle/resolve the differences; smooth/iron out the differences</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>discrepancy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разногласие.html>разногла́сие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:показание.html>показа́ниях</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raznoglásije</b> v pokazánijax</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">conflicting evidence</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
